#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0017 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x0018 [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  2: 0x001A [0x5D] SET_MUSIC_VOLUME(volume=0*, fade_time=300*)
  3: 0x001F [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK: Load scheduler "fdo1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=[200*, 0*]
  4: 0x0030 [0x55] WAIT_LOAD_SCHEDULER: Wait for scheduler "fdo1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=200*
  5: 0x003F [0x38] SET_CLIENT_EVENT_MODE(mode=19*)
  6: 0x0042 [0x2F] DIRECTOR2 (ID: 17924188/0x0111805C)->Render.Flags0 &= ~0x80000 // Bit 19
  7: 0x0048 [0x29] REQ_SET_WAIT(priority=0x08, entity_id=DIRECTOR2 (ID: 17924188/0x0111805C), tag_num=0x1E)
```
